<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paal.html>paal</a> (5995)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pâel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">pāl</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pālus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paal.html>paal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:palen.html>palen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paaltje.html>paaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>post, <a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>stake</a>, pole, pile</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> goalpost
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doelpaal.html>doelpaal</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pale, perpendicular stripe</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> erect phallus</li>
<li>an Indonesian measure of distance</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paard.html>paard</a> (914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pert</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pāert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*pered</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">paraverēdus</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pferd</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paard.html>paard</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paarden.html>paarden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paardje.html>paardje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A horse, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:equus.html>Equus</a> caballus</i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:equus.html>Equus</a> ferus</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A knight.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">gymnastics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pommel horse.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A rope hanging beneath a spar or other horizontal beam, often fixed in place by other ropes.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An ugly woman.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">animal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ros.html>ros</a></span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paarde.html>paarde</a> (80574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paarde.html>paarde</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"> singular past indicative and subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paren.html>paren</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:paarde.html>paarde</a></b>
</p>

***paars.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paars.html>paars</a> (9302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">paers</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">peers</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pers.html>pers</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">purple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:pers.html>pers</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blue-grey, dark <a href = vnd.unilang:violet.html>violet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">persus</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">persum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dark blue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Possibly derived from either <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Persae</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Persians</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Persia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Persia</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, referring to the colour of a garment, or from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">persica</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, referring to the colour of peach blossom.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paars.html>paars</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paars.html>paarser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paars.html>paars</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">paarst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>purple</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> relating to cooperation between liberals and social democrats of the third way <span class="defdate">[from late 20th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bruinpaars</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">pimpelpaars</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paars.html>paars</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The colour purple.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A coalition of third way social democrats and liberals. <span class="defdate">[from late 20th c.]</span></li></ol>

***pad.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pad.html>pad</a> (1571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">path</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*paþaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">path</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">path</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">paad</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pfad</i>.

***paddy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a> (14610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">padi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a> plant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">paddies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Rough or unhusked rice, either before it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> milled or as a crop to be harvested. <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>2011</b>, Deepika Phukan, translating <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arupa_Patangia_Kalita" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Arupa Patangia Kalita">Arupa Patangia Kalita</a>, <i>The Story of Felanee</i>:
<dl><dd>Taking out a handful of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></b> the old woman exclaimed, “Look how good this <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>! It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called Malbhog – it <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> excellent puffed rice.”</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a> field, a rice <a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a>; an irrigated or flooded field where rice <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> grown. <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>English dialect <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">worm-eaten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Low; mean; boorish; vagabond.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Digges to this entry?)</span></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by John Lothrop Motley and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> after the expiration of four months the condition of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></b> persons continued most destitute. The English <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>soldiers</a> became <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a> barefoot starving beggars in the streets<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>Paddy</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Irishman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">paddies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fit of temper; a tantrum
<dl><dd><i>throw a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></b></i> etc.</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2013</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mike.html>Mike</a> Brown, <i>Adventures with Czech George</i> (page 17)
<dl><dd>I like the story of the Emperor Frederick who got into a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paddy.html>paddy</a></b> with his cook, and shouted: 'I am the Emperor, and I want <a href = vnd.unilang:dumplings.html>dumplings</a>.'</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/African-American_Vernacular_English" class="extiw" title="w:African-American Vernacular English">African-American Vernacular</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A white person.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/England" class="extiw" title="w:England">England</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A labourer's assistant or workmate.</li>
<li>A drill used in boring wells, with <a href = vnd.unilang:cutters.html>cutters</a> that expand on pressure.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:paella.html>paella</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catalan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Catalan language">Catalan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ca"><a href = vnd.unilang:paella.html>paella</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a>; pan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">paelle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">patella</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plate, small pan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">patella</i> and possibly <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pail</i>.
</p>

***pakkans.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pakkans.html>pakkans</a> (89561)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakken.html>pakken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kans.html>kans</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakkans.html>pakkans</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakkans.html>pakkansen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakkans.html>pakkansje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law enforcement</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> probability of apprehension; probability of arresting the criminal guilty of a crime
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, Henriëtte Prast, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>Geld</a> amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:gevoel.html>gevoel</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:emoties.html>emoties</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ethiek.html>ethiek</a></i>, Atlas Contact.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pakken.html>pakken</a> (607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">packen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pak.html>pak</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakken.html>pakke</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take, <a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakje.html>pakje</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grab, take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">packen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grab</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***paladin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paladin.html>paladin</a> (89560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:paladin.html>paladin</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">paladino</i>, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">بالادين</i> |  from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">palatinus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">palace officer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">palatium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">palace</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">palatine</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paladin.html>paladin</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paladins.html>paladins</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A heroic champion (especially a knightly one).</li>
<li>A defender or advocate of a noble cause. (A defender of faith).</li>
<li>Any of the twelve Companions of the court of Emperor Charlemagne.</li></ol>
</body>

***palaver.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a> (53558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally nautical <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">palavra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">word</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">parabola</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">parable, speech</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The term's use (especially in Africa) mimics the evolution of the word moot. As such, for sense development, see moot. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">parable</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">parole</i><span class="serial-comma">,</span><span class="serial-and"> and</span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">parabola</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">palavers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Africa</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A village council meeting.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1799</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mungo_Park_(explorer)" class="extiw" title="w:Mungo Park (explorer)"><a href = vnd.unilang:mungo.html>Mungo</a> Park</a>,  <cite>Travels in the Interior of Africa</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=ByYAAAAAQAAJamp;pg=PA340amp;dq=%22Here+we+remained+four+days,+on+account+of+a+palaver+which+was+held+on+the+following+occasion.%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=ffkxTqHDKoO50AGw3-GADAamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=8amp;ved=0CEwQ6AEwBwv=onepageamp;q=%22Here%20we%20remained%20four%20days%2C%20on%20account%20of%20a%20palaver%20which%20was%20held%20on%20the%20following%20occasion.%22amp;f=false">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Here <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> remained four days, on account of a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></b> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> on the following occasion.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Talk, especially unnecessary talk; chatter.
<ul><li><b>1886</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_James" class="extiw" title="w:Henry James"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> James</a>, <i>The Princess Casamassima</i>.
<dl><dd>These remarks <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> received with a differing demonstration: some of the company declaring that if the <a href = vnd.unilang:dutchman.html>Dutchman</a> cared to come round and smoke a pipe they would be glad to see him—perhaps he'd show where the thumbscrews <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> put on; others being strongly of the opinion that they didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> want any more advice—they <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> already <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> advice enough to turn a donkey's stomach. What they <a href = vnd.unilang:wanted.html>wanted</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> to put forth their might without any more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></b>; to do something, or for some one; to go out somewhere and smash something, on the spot—why not?—that very night.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1899</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Crane" class="extiw" title="w:Stephen Crane">Stephen Crane</a>, <i>Active Service</i>:
<dl><dd>Knowing full well the right time and the wrong time for a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></b> of regret and disavowal, this battalion struggled in the desperation of despair.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1979</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V._S._Naipaul" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:V. S. Naipaul">V. S. Naipaul</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Bend_in_the_River" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Bend in the River">A Bend in the River</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Some of the <b>palavers</b> could take <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a day.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1985</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Justin_Richards" class="extiw" title="w:Justin Richards">Justin Richards</a>, <i>Option Lock</i>, p 229:
<dl><dd>Not for the first time, he reflected that it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not so much the <a href = vnd.unilang:speeches.html>speeches</a> that strained the nerves as the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> with them.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Talk intended to deceive.</li>
<li>Fuss.
<dl><dd><i>What a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></b>!</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A meeting at which there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> much talk; a debate; a moot.
<ul><li><b>1851</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Carlyle" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Thomas Carlyle">Thomas Carlyle</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Life_of_John_Sterling" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Life of John Sterling">The Life of John Sterling</a></i>
<dl><dd>this country and epoch of parliaments and eloquent <b>palavers</b></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Disagreement.
<dl><dd><i>I have no <b><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></b> with him.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">unnecessary talk</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hot air</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">janglery</span>; See also Thesaurus:chatter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fuss</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">ado</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">bother</span>; See also Thesaurus:commotion</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">palavers</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">palavering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">palavered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To discuss with much talk.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moby_Dick" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Moby Dick"><a href = vnd.unilang:moby.html>Moby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>Dick</a></a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/ebooks/2701">[2]</a></sup>, chapter 21:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“Come, come, <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a> Bildad; <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> <b>palavering</b>,—away!” and with that, Peleg hurried him <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the side, and both <a href = vnd.unilang:dropt.html>dropt</a> into the boat.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1860</b>, <i>Atlantic Monthly</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 5, no. 30 (April),
<dl><dd>“That,” he rejoined, “is a way <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> Americans have. <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> cannot <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:palaver.html>palaver</a></b>. What would become of our manifest destiny?”</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>To flatter.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">jabber</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rabbit</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yak.html>yak</a></span>; See also Thesaurus:prattle</li></ul>
<hr />

</p>

***paleis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paleis.html>paleis</a> (3410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:palais.html>palais</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:palais.html>palais</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">palātium</i>.
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:palissade.html>palissade</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">palissada</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">palissa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>stake</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">pal</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>stake</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or possibly a from Gallo-Romance <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*pālīcea</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pālus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>stake</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisades.html>palisades</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A long, strong <a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>stake</a>, one end of which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> set firmly in the ground, and the other sharpened.</li>
<li>A wall of wooden stakes, used as a defensive barrier.</li>
<li>A line of cliffs, especially one showing basaltic <a href = vnd.unilang:columns.html>columns</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> row of cells. e.g.: <a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a> mesophyll cells.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a> worm</span></li>
<li>palisadic</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisades.html>palisades</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">palisading</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">palisaded</b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paljas.html>paljas</a> (37890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">paillasse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">palea</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paljas.html>paljas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paljassen.html>paljassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paljas.html>paljasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sack of straw, a paillasse.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">paillasse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">pagliaccio</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">palea</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">pias</i>. Compare to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pierrot.html>Pierrot</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">buffoon</span>, a <a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hansworst.html>hansworst</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">pias</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sul.html>sul</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zot.html>zot</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
